###########################
# Annexation Events 151-300
###########################
# By lots of folks
# Converted from on_actions to decisions by Rylock and Dr_Njitram
# Any new post-annexation events need to have their triggers in the KR_on_actions file
###########################

add_namespace = annex

country_event = { #Liberation of Montenegro
	id = annex.151
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.151" }
	title = annexation_MNT_CONQ
	desc = annexation_MNT_CONQ_desc

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #liberate
		name = annex.151.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = MNT }
		release_targeted_tag = yes
	}
	option = { #Give it to Austria
		name = annex.150.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				AUS = { is_ally_of_ROOT = no }
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			AUS = {
				AUS_is_unified = yes
				owns_state = 163
				is_ally_of_ROOT = yes
			}
			NOT = {
				tag = CRO
				tag = AUS
			}
		}
		105 = {
			if = {
				limit = { is_claimed_by = AUS }
				remove_claim_by = AUS
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { is_core_of = AUS } }
				add_core_of = AUS
			}
			AUS = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}
	option = { #Give it to Croatia
		name = annex.150.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		trigger = {
			CRO = {
				is_ally_of_ROOT = yes
				owns_state = 163
			}
			NOT = {
				tag = CRO
				AND = {
					tag = AUS
					AUS_is_unified = yes
				}
			}
		}
		105 = {
			if = {
				limit = { is_claimed_by = CRO }
				remove_claim_by = CRO
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { is_core_of = CRO } }
				add_core_of = CRO
			}
			CRO = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}
	option = { #Give it to Serbia
		name = annex.150.d
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 300
		}
		trigger = {
			SER = { is_ally_of_ROOT = yes }
			NOT = {
				tag = CRO
				AND = {
					tag = AUS
					AUS_is_unified = yes
				}
			}
		}
		105 = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						is_claimed_by = SER
						is_core_of = SER
					}
				}
				add_claim_by = SER
			}
			SER = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}
	option = { #annex
		name = annex.17.h
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				tag = CRO
				AND = {
					tag = AUS
					AUS_is_unified = yes
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1000
		}
		105 = {
			if = {
				limit = { is_claimed_by = ROOT }
				remove_claim_by = ROOT
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { is_core_of = ROOT } }
				add_core_of = ROOT
			}
		}
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}
	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.occupation
		trigger = {
			is_ai = no
			NOT = {
				tag = CRO
				tag = SER
				AND = {
					tag = AUS
					AUS_is_unified = yes
				}
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = MNT_CONQ
		occupy_small_country = yes
	}
}

country_event = { #Albania Liberation
	id = annex.152
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.152" }
	title = annexation_ALB_CONQ
	desc = annexation_ALB_CONQ_desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			add_to_temp_array = { core_removal_array = ALB }
			remove_all_cores_and_claims_of_tags = yes
			44 = { add_core_of = ALB }
		}
	}

	option = { #liberate
		name = annex.152.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				AND = {
					tag = AUS
					ALB = {
						NOT = { has_country_flag = ALB_wieddead }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = ALB }
		release_targeted_tag = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			765 = { add_core_of = ALB }
			766 = { add_core_of = ALB }
		}
	}
	option = { #liberate for austria (wied option)
		name = annex.152.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
		}
		trigger = {
			tag = AUS
			ALB = {
				NOT = { has_country_flag = ALB_wieddead }
			}
		}

		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = ALB }
		release_targeted_tag = yes

		ALB = {
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Wilhelm zu Wied"
				desc = "POLITICS_WILLIAM_WIED_DESC"
				picture = "Portrait_Albania_Wilhelm_Wied.tga"
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = authoritarian_democrat_subtype
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = authoritarian_democrat
				long_name = "Grafschaft Wied-Neuwied"
				name = "Grafschaft Wied-Neuwied"
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = authoritarian_democrat
				popularity = 0.4
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = authoritarian_democrat
				elections_allowed = no
			}
			set_country_flag = ALB_restoration_of_wied
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			765 = { add_core_of = ALB }
			766 = { add_core_of = ALB }
		}
	}
	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.occupation
		trigger = { is_ai = no }
		set_country_flag = ALB_CONQ
		occupy_small_country = yes
	}
}

country_event = { #Netherlands Liberation
	id = annex.154
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.154" }
	title = annexation_HOL_CONQ
	desc = annexation_HOL_CONQ_desc
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			HOL = { drop_cosmetic_tag = yes }
		}
	}

	option = { #liberate
		name = annex.154.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				tag = BEL
				OR = {
					has_government = national_populist
					has_government = paternal_autocrat
				}
			}
		}

		HOL = {
			add_state_core = 979
			add_state_core = 978
		}

		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = HOL }
		release_targeted_tag = yes

		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction_with = DEI
			}
			country_event = holex.41
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { tag = GER }
			country_event = hol.4
		}
	}

	option = { #Restore to the government in exile
		name = annex.154.f
		trigger = {
			is_in_faction_with = DEI
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 160
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { owns_state = 978 }
				HOL = { add_state_core = 978 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { owns_state = 979 }
				HOL = { add_state_core = 979 }
			}
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = HOL
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}
			DEI = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #liberate but give Limburg and Zeeuws-Vlaanderen to Belgium/Flanders-Wallonia
		name = annex.154.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 80
		}
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					country_exists = BEL
					OR = {
						tag = BEL
						is_in_faction_with = BEL
					}
				}
				AND = {
					country_exists = FLN
					OR = {
						tag = FLN
						is_in_faction_with = FLN
					}
				}
			}
			OR = {
				978 = {
					is_owned_by = ROOT
				}
				979 = {
					is_owned_by = ROOT
				}
			}
		}

		978 = {
			remove_core_of = HOL
		}
		979 = {
			remove_core_of = HOL
		}

		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = HOL }
		release_targeted_tag = yes

		if = {
			limit = {
				978 = {
					is_owned_by = ROOT
				}
				NOT = {
					AND = {
						OR = {
							tag = FRA
							tag = NFA
							tag = BEL
							tag = WLL
							tag = FLN
							AND = {
								is_german_tag = yes
								781 = { is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes } #Western Rhineland
							}
						}
						6 = { is_claimed_by = ROOT } #Flanders
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					country_exists = BEL
				}
				BEL = {
					transfer_state = 978
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					WLL = {
						owns_state = 6
					}
				}
				WLL = {
					transfer_state = 978
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					country_exists = FLN
				}
				FLN = {
					transfer_state = 978
				}
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				979 = {
					is_owned_by = ROOT
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					country_exists = BEL
				}
				BEL = {
					transfer_state = 979
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					WLL = {
						owns_state = 6
					}
				}
				WLL = {
					transfer_state = 979
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					country_exists = FLN
				}
				FLN = {
					transfer_state = 979
				}
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction_with = DEI
			}
			country_event = holex.41
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { tag = GER }
			country_event = hol.4
		}
	}

	option = { #liberate but keep Limbourg
		name = annex.154.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 80
		}
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				tag = GER
				tag = GRU #For the future
			}
		}

		978 = {
			remove_core_of = HOL
		}

		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = HOL }
		release_targeted_tag = yes

		country_event = {
			id = hol.4
			days = 2
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction_with = DEI
			}
			country_event = holex.41
		}
	}

	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.154.e
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 80
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = {
					AND = {
						tag = BEL
						OR = {
							has_government = national_populist
							has_government = paternal_autocrat
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = HOL_CONQ
		occupy_medium_country = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction_with = DEI
			}
			country_event = holex.41
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Denmark Liberation
	id = annex.155
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.155" }
	title = annexation_DEN_CONQ
	desc = annexation_DEN_CONQ_desc
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #liberate as monarchy
		name = annex.155.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 98

		}
		trigger = {
			has_socialist_government = no
			NOT = {
				has_government = national_populist
			}
		}

		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = DEN }
		release_targeted_tag = yes

		DEN = {
			clr_country_flag = den_hybrid
			clr_country_flag = den_danish_republic
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			DEN = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						date < 1947.05.20
					}
					create_country_leader = {
						name = "Christian X"
						desc = "CHRISTIAN_X_DESC"
						picture = "Portrait_Denmark_Christian_X.tga"
						expire = "1965.1.1"
						ideology = social_conservative_subtype
					}
					create_country_leader = {
						name = "Christian X"
						desc = "CHRISTIAN_X_DESC"
						picture = "Portrait_Denmark_Christian_X.tga"
						expire = "1965.1.1"
						ideology = authoritarian_democrat_subtype
					}
					create_country_leader = {
						name = "Christian X"
						desc = "CHRISTIAN_X_DESC"
						picture = "Portrait_Denmark_Christian_X.tga"
						expire = "1965.1.1"
						ideology = social_democrat_subtype
					}
					create_country_leader = {
						name = "Christian X"
						desc = "CHRISTIAN_X_DESC"
						picture = "Portrait_Denmark_Christian_X.tga"
						expire = "1965.1.1"
						ideology = paternal_autocrat_subtype
					}
					create_country_leader = {
						name = "Christian X"
						desc = "CHRISTIAN_X_DESC"
						picture = "Portrait_Denmark_Christian_X.tga"
						expire = "1965.1.1"
						ideology = market_liberal_subtype
					}
					create_country_leader = {
						name = "Christian X"
						desc = "CHRISTIAN_X_DESC"
						picture = "Portrait_Denmark_Christian_X.tga"
						expire = "1965.1.1"
						ideology = social_liberal_subtype
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						date > 1947.05.20
					}
					create_country_leader = {
						name = "Frederick IX"
						picture = "Portrait_Denmark_Frederick.tga"
						expire = "1965.1.1"
						ideology = social_democrat_subtype
					}
					create_country_leader = {
						name = "Frederick IX"
						picture = "Portrait_Denmark_Frederick.tga"
						expire = "1965.1.1"
						ideology = social_liberal_subtype
					}
					create_country_leader = {
						name = "Frederick IX"
						picture = "Portrait_Denmark_Frederick.tga"
						expire = "1965.1.1"
						ideology = market_liberal_subtype
					}
					create_country_leader = {
						name = "Frederick IX"
						picture = "Portrait_Denmark_Frederick.tga"
						expire = "1965.1.1"
						ideology = social_conservative_subtype
					}
					create_country_leader = {
						name = "Frederick IX"
						picture = "Portrait_Denmark_Frederick.tga"
						expire = "1965.1.1"
						ideology = authoritarian_democrat_subtype
					}
					create_country_leader = {
						name = "Frederick IX"
						picture = "Portrait_Denmark_Frederick.tga"
						expire = "1965.1.1"
						ideology = paternal_autocrat_subtype
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #liberate as republic
		name = annex.155.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 98

		}
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				tag = GER
				tag = AUS
			}
		}

		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = DEN }
		release_targeted_tag = yes

		DEN = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_socialist_government = yes
					}
				}
				clr_country_flag = den_hybrid
			}
			set_country_flag = den_danish_republic
		}

		hidden_effect = {
			DEN = {
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Thorvald Stauning"
					picture = "Portrait_Denmark_Thorvald_Stauning_kr.tga"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = social_democrat_subtype
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Peter Munch"
					picture = "Portrait_Denmark_Peter_Munch.tga"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = social_liberal_subtype
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Thomas Madsen-Mygdal"
					picture = "Portrait_Denmark_Thomas_Madsen_Mygdal.tga"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = market_liberal_subtype
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "John Christmas Møller"
					picture = "Portrait_Denmark_Christmas_Moller.tga"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = social_conservative_subtype
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Erik With"
					picture = "Portrait_Denmark_Erik_With.tga"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = authoritarian_democrat_subtype
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Christian von Schalburg"
					picture = "Portrait_Denmark_Christian_von_Schalburg.tga"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = paternal_autocrat_subtype
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.occupation
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		set_country_flag = DEN_CONQ
		occupy_medium_country = yes
	}
}

country_event = { #Fate of Portugal
	id = annex.156
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.156" }
	title = annexation_POR_CONQ
	desc = annexation_POR_CONQ_desc
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Liberate a republican Portugal
		name = annex.156.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				tag = SWF
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = { country_exists = POR }
				OR = {
					is_german_tag = yes
					tag = CAN
					tag = GBR
					tag = NFA
					tag = SPA
					tag = SPR
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { country_exists = POR }
			custom_effect_tooltip = POR_puppet_tooltip
			hidden_effect = {
				create_dynamic_country = {
					original_tag = POR
					copy_tag = POR
					create_country_leader = {
						name = "Bento António Gonçalves"
						picture = "gfx/leaders/POR/Portrait_Portugal_Bento_Goncalves.tga"
						expire = "1965.1.1"
						ideology = totalist_subtype
					}
					create_country_leader = {
						name = "Manuel Joaquim de Sousa"
						picture = "gfx/leaders/Generic/Portrait_Europe_Generic_new_3.tga"
						expire = "1965.1.1"
						ideology = syndicalist_subtype
					}
					create_country_leader = {
						name = "Amílcar Ramada Curto"
						picture = "gfx/leaders/POR/Portrait_POR_Amilcar_Ramada_Curto.tga"
						expire = "1965.1.1"
						ideology = radical_socialist_subtype
					}
					create_country_leader = {
						name = "José Domingues dos Santos"
						picture = "gfx/leaders/POR/Portrait_POR_José_Domingues_dos_Santos.tga"
						expire = "1965.1.1"
						ideology = social_democrat_subtype
					}
					create_country_leader = {
						name = "Liberato Pinto"
						picture = "gfx/leaders/POR/Portrait_POR_Liberato_Pinto.tga"
						expire = "1965.1.1"
						ideology = social_liberal_subtype
					}
					create_country_leader = {
						name = "Antonio Granjo"
						picture = "gfx/leaders/POR/Portrait_Portugal_Antonio_Granjo.tga"
						expire = "1965.1.1"
						ideology = market_liberal_subtype
					}
					create_country_leader = {
						name = "Francisco da Cunha Leal"
						picture = "gfx/leaders/POR/Portrait_POR_Francisco_da_Cunha_Leal.tga"
						expire = "1965.1.1"
						ideology = social_conservative_subtype
					}
					create_country_leader = {
						name = "Antonio de Oliveira Salazar"
						picture = "gfx/leaders/POR/Portrait_Portugal_Antonio_Carmona.tga"
						expire = "1965.1.1"
						ideology = paternal_autocrat_subtype
					}
					create_country_leader = {
						name = "Antonio Oscar Fragoso Carmona"
						picture = "gfx/leaders/POR/Portrait_Portugal_Antonio_Carmona.tga"
						expire = "1965.1.1"
						ideology = paternal_autocrat_subtype
					}
					create_country_leader = {
						name = "Francisco Rolão Preto"
						picture = "gfx/leaders/POR/Portrait_POR_Francisco_Rolao_Preto.tga"
						expire = "1965.1.1"
						ideology = national_populist_subtype
					}
					set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = THIS }
				}
				add_to_temp_array = { target_cores_to_release = POR }
				release_targeted_tag_from_core_regions = yes
				var:tag_to_release = { set_cosmetic_tag = RPO }
			}
		}
		else = {
			set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = POR }
			release_targeted_tag = yes
			var:tag_to_release = {
				remove_portuguese_monarchy = yes
				set_cosmetic_tag = RPO
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Restore the Portuguese monarchy
		name = annex.156.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = { country_exists = POR }
			has_socialist_government = no
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_german_tag = no
				NOT = {
					tag = CAN
					tag = GBR
					tag = NFA
					tag = SPA

country_event = { #Fate of France
	id = annex.157
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.157" }
	title = annexation_FRA_CONQ
	desc = annexation_FRA_CONQ_desc
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = annex.157.a #Restore the Commune of France!
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1000
		}
		trigger = {
			has_socialist_government = yes
			NOT = { country_exists = FRA }
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = FRA }
		release_france = yes
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction = yes
				is_faction_leader = yes
			}
			set_autonomy = {
				target = FRA
				autonomy_state = autonomy_free
			}
			add_to_faction = FRA
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = annex.157.b #Restore National France!
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1000
		}
		trigger = {
			is_ally_with = ENT
			NOT = { country_exists = NFA }
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = NFA }
		release_france = yes
		set_autonomy = {
			target = var:tag_to_release
			autonomy_state = autonomy_free
		}
		ENT = { add_to_faction = NFA }
	}

	option = {
		name = annex.157.c #Set up a French Puppet Government
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90
		}
		trigger = {
			has_socialist_government = no
			NOT = {
				is_ally_with = ENT
				is_ally_with = NFA
				country_exists = FRP
				AND = {
					tag = GER
					NFA = {
						any_owned_state = {
							is_european_france = yes
							NOT = { state = 1 } #Corsica doesn't count
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = FRP }
		release_france = yes
	}

	option = {
		name = annex.157.d #Give it to our French allies
		trigger = {
			is_ally_with = NFA
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1000
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_european_france = yes
				if = {
					limit = {
						ROOT = { is_italian_tag = yes }
					}
					NOT = {
						state = 762 #Nice
						state = 735 #Savoy
						state = 943 #Upper Savoy
					}
				}
			}
			NFA = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = annex.157.e #Meet with the French
		trigger = {
			AND = {
				NFA = {
					any_owned_state = {
						NOT = { state = 1 } #Corsica doesn't count
						is_european_france = yes
					}
				}
				tag = GER
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1000
		}
		NFA = { country_event = { id = nfa.120 } }
	}

	option = {
		name = annex.occupation
		trigger = { is_ai = no }
		if = {
			limit = { country_exists = NFA }

				target = NFA

			}
		}

	}
}

				add_state_core = 948 #Liège
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { tag = GER }
					741 = {
						is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
						is_clear_other_claims = yes
					}
				}
				WLL = { add_state_core = 741 } #Wallonian Luxembourg
			}
		}

		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = WLL
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}
			FLN = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
	}

	option = { #Give Wallonia to Belgium
		name = annex.162.f
		trigger = {
			is_ally_with = BEL
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 200
		}

		hidden_effect = {
			add_to_temp_array = { core_removal_array = WLL }
			remove_all_cores_and_claims_of_tags = yes
		}

		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 34 #Hainaut
					state = 741 #Wallonian Luxembourg
					state = 948 #Liège
				}
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_claimed_by = BEL }
				remove_claim_by = BEL
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { is_core_of = BEL } }
				add_core_of = BEL
			}
			BEL = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
	}

	option = { #Annex Wallonia
		name = annex.162.g
		trigger = {
			is_french_tag = yes
			owns_state = 16
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				tag = NFA
			}
		}
		add_state_claim = 34
		add_state_claim = 741
		add_state_claim = 948
		set_country_flag = WLL_CONQ
		occupy_medium_country = yes
	}

	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.occupation
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				AND = {
					is_french_tag = yes
					owns_state = 16
				}
				AND = {
					tag = FLN
					NOT = { country_exists = BEL }
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		set_country_flag = WLL_CONQ
		occupy_small_country = yes
	}
}

			}
		}
		set_country_flag = INC_CONQ
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}

		name = annex.170.c

			factor = 100
		}
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				tag = GER
				tag = GEX
			}
			country_exists = GEA
		}

			limit = {

					is_core_of = VIN

					is_core_of = LAO

			if = {
				limit = { is_claimed_by = GEA }

				add_core_of = GEA

			GEA = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}

	option = { #occupy

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		occupy_medium_country = yes
		set_country_flag = INC_CONQ

							state = 734

							NOT = {

			}

						market_liberal = 8
						social_conservative = 3
						authoritarian_democrat = 12

				}

				}

					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = social_conservative
					}
					set_popularities = {
						totalist = 0
						radical_socialist = 0
						syndicalist = 0
						social_democrat = 2
						social_liberal = 10
						market_liberal = 8
						social_conservative = 63
						authoritarian_democrat = 12
						paternal_autocrat = 3

						radical_socialist = 0

						social_democrat = 2
						social_liberal = 23
						market_liberal = 28
						social_conservative = 13
						authoritarian_democrat = 12

				limit = {
					is_brazil = yes
					NOT = {
						state = 855 #Acre
						state = 1040 #Acre Jungle
						state = 1041 #Iguassu
						state = 1043 #Ponta Pora
					}
				}
				add_core_of = BRA
			}
		}

		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = BRA }
		release_targeted_tag = yes

		hidden_effect = {
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_brazil = yes
					NOT = { is_core_of = BRA }
				}
				add_core_of = BRA
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { country_exists = PIR }
				}
				event_target:BRA_Setembrino_de_Carvalho = { set_nationality = BRA }
				event_target:BRA_Jose_Leite_de_Castro = { set_nationality = BRA }
				event_target:BRA_Nelson_de_Mello = { set_nationality = BRA }
				event_target:BRA_Mascarenhas_de_Morais = { set_nationality = BRA }
				event_target:BRA_Sezefredo_Passos = { set_nationality = BRA }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { country_exists = SPO }
				}
				event_target:BRA_Isidoro_Dias_Lopes = { set_nationality = BRA }
				event_target:BRA_Euclides_Figueiredo = { set_nationality = BRA }
				event_target:BRA_Bertoldo_Klinger = { set_nationality = BRA }
				event_target:BRA_Julio_Marcondes_Salgado = { set_nationality = BRA }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { country_exists = RJM }
				}
				event_target:BRA_Newton_Estillac_Leal = { set_nationality = BRA }
				event_target:BRA_Araken_de_Oliveira = { set_nationality = BRA }
				event_target:BRA_Horta_Barbosa = { set_nationality = BRA }
				event_target:BRA_Olimpio_Mourao_Filho = { set_nationality = BRA }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { country_exists = GOY }
				}
				event_target:BRA_Candido_Rondon = { set_nationality = BRA }
				event_target:BRA_Euclides_Zenobio_da_Costa = { set_nationality = BRA }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { country_exists = GRP }
				}
				event_target:BRA_Newton_Cavalcanti = { set_nationality = BRA }
				event_target:BRA_Castelo_Branco = { set_nationality = BRA }
				event_target:BRA_Gois_Monteiro = { set_nationality = BRA }
				event_target:BRA_Tertuliano_Potiguara = { set_nationality = BRA }
			}

			if = {
				limit = { has_government = national_populist }
				BRA = {
					load_focus_tree = {
						tree = Brazil_Focus_Imperial
						keep_completed = yes
					}
					complete_national_focus = BRA_AIB
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_government = paternal_autocrat }
				BRA = {
					load_focus_tree = {
						tree = Brazil_Focus_Vargas
						keep_completed = yes
					}
					complete_national_focus = BRA_new_state
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_government = authoritarian_democrat
						has_democratic_government = yes
					}
				}
				BRA = {
					load_focus_tree = {
						tree = Brazil_Focus_Democratic
						keep_completed = yes
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_government = radical_socialist
						AND = {
							has_government = social_democrat
							has_country_flag = soc_dems_are_socialists
						}
					}
				}
				BRA = {
					load_focus_tree = {
						tree = Brazil_Focus_Anarchist
						keep_completed = yes
					}
					complete_national_focus = BRA_the_counter_coup
					complete_national_focus = BRA_f_anarchist_b
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_government = syndicalist }
				BRA = {
					load_focus_tree = {
						tree = Brazil_Focus_Syndicalist
						keep_completed = yes
					}
					complete_national_focus = BRA_the_counter_coup
					complete_national_focus = BRA_syndicalist_alliance
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_government = totalist }
				BRA = {
					load_focus_tree = {
						tree = Brazil_Focus_Totalist
						keep_completed = yes
					}
					complete_national_focus = BRA_the_counter_coup
					complete_national_focus = BRA_ato_institucional_1
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Balkanise Brazil
		name = annex.181.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				tag = ARG
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = BRA_CONQ
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}

	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.occupation
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		occupy_medium_country = yes
		set_country_flag = BRA_CONQ
		set_country_flag = PIR_CONQ
		set_country_flag = SPO_CONQ
		set_country_flag = RJM_CONQ
		set_country_flag = GOY_CONQ
		set_country_flag = BAH_CONQ
		set_country_flag = GRP_CONQ
		set_country_flag = AMA_CONQ
	}
}

country_event = { #Fate of Argentina
	id = annex.182
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.182" }
	title = annexation_ARG_CONQ
	desc = annexation_ARG_CONQ_desc

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						tag = ENT
						tag = GBR
					}
				}
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
						OR = {
							state = 299 #Falklands
							state = 720 #South Georgia Islands
						}
					}
					add_claim_by = ROOT
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { tag = PAR }
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
						OR = {
							state = 901 #Chaco Austral
							state = 1074 #Corrientes
						}
					}
					add_claim_by = ROOT
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { tag = BOL }
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
						is_core_of = ARG
						OR = {
							region = 204 #Gran Chaco
							state = 903 #Jujuy
						}
					}
					add_claim_by = ROOT
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { tag = CHL }
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
						is_core_of = ARG
						OR = {
							state = 512 #Chubut
							state = 1028 #Tierra del Fuego
							state = 1029 #Santa Cruz
						}
					}
					add_claim_by = ROOT
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_democratic_government = no }
				ARG = {
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = var:current_party_ideology_group
						elections_allowed = no
					}
				}
			}
			901 = { remove_core_of = ARG }
			1074 = { remove_core_of = ARG }
			901 = { remove_core_of = FOP }
			1074 = { remove_core_of = FOP }
		}
	}

	option = { #liberate full argentina
		name = annex.182.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 70
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				tag = BRA
				has_government = national_populist
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				is_ally_with = ARG
				is_ally_with = FOP
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_socialist_government = yes }
			set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = FOP }
		}
		else = {
			set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = ARG }
		}
		add_to_temp_array = { target_cores_to_release = ARG }
		add_to_temp_array = { target_cores_to_release = FOP }
		release_targeted_tag_from_core_regions = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = BRA
				has_government = national_populist
			}
			ARG = {
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Miguel de Andrea"
					desc = "POLITICS_MIGUEL_DE_ANDREA_DESC"
					picture = "Portrait_Argentine_miguel_de_andrea.tga"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = national_populist_subtype
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { ARG = { owns_state = 278 } }
				901 = { add_core_of = ARG }
				1074 = { add_core_of = ARG }
			}
			else = {
				901 = { add_core_of = FOP }
				1074 = { add_core_of = FOP }
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Liberate argentina and patagonia
		name = annex.182.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
		}
		trigger = {
			tag = BRA
			has_government = national_populist
			owns_state = 512
			NOT = { country_exists = FOP }
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			add_to_temp_array = { core_removal_array = FOP }
			remove_all_cores_and_claims_of_tags = yes
			FOP = {
				add_state_core = 507 #Magallanes
				add_state_core = 512 #Chubut
				add_state_core = 1028 #Tierra del Fuego
				add_state_core = 1029 #Santa Cruz
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = FOP }
		release_targeted_tag = yes
		var:tag_to_release = {
			FOP_remove_all_ideas = yes
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Antoine III"
				picture = "Portrait_FOP_Jacques_Antoine_Bernard.tga"
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = national_populist_subtype
			}
			if = {
				limit = { owns_state = 507 } #Magallanes
				hidden_effect = { set_capital = 507 }
			}
		}

		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = ARG }
		release_targeted_tag = yes
		var:tag_to_release = {
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Miguel de Andrea"
				desc = "POLITICS_MIGUEL_DE_ANDREA_DESC"
				picture = "Portrait_Argentine_miguel_de_andrea.tga"
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = national_populist_subtype
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			901 = { add_core_of = ARG }
			1074 = { add_core_of = ARG }
		}
	}

	option = { #Give to FOP
		name = annex.182.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		trigger = {
			is_ally_with = FOP
		}
		add_to_temp_array = { target_cores_to_release = ARG }
		add_to_temp_array = { target_cores_to_release = FOP }
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = FOP }
		transfer_territory_from_core_regions = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			901 = { add_core_of = FOP }
			1074 = { add_core_of = FOP }
		}
	}

	option = { #occupy

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}

		}

		set_country_flag = ARG_CONQ
	}

country_event = { #Annexation of Mozambique
	id = annex.191
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.191" }
	title = annexation_MZB_CONQ
	desc = annexation_MZB_CONQ_desc
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #liberate
		name = annex.191.a
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = MZB }
		release_targeted_tag = yes
	}

	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.occupation
		trigger = { is_ai = no }
		set_country_flag = MZB_CONQ
		occupy_medium_country = yes
	}
}

country_event = { #Fate of Somalia

	id = annex.192
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.192" }
	title = annexation_SOM_CONQ
	desc = annexation_SOM_CONQ_desc
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					tag = NFA
					owns_state = 268 #Djibouti
				}
				add_state_claim = 268
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #SOM
		name = annex.192.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_core_of = SOM
					AND = {
						state = 944 #Harar
						NOT = {
							ROOT = { owns_state = 271 } #Can release Ethiopia
							any_country = {
								is_ally_of_ROOT = yes
								PREV = { is_claim_or_core_of_PREV = yes }
							}
						}
					}
					AND = {
						state = 892 #Jubaland
						NOT = {
							ROOT = { owns_state = 970 } #Can release Kenya
							any_country = {
								is_ally_of_ROOT = yes
								PREV = { is_claim_or_core_of_PREV = yes }
							}
						}
					}
				}
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}
			SOM = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}

		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = SOM }
		puppet_released_tag = yes
	}

	option = { #occupation

		name = annex.192.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}

		set_country_flag = SOM_CONQ

		occupy_medium_country = yes
	}
}

country_event = { #Annexation of Namibia
	id = annex.193
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.193" }
	title = annexation_NMB_CONQ
	desc = annexation_NMB_CONQ_desc
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			add_to_temp_array = { core_removal_array = PAR }
			remove_all_cores_and_claims_of_tags = yes
			NMB = {
				add_state_core = 541 #South West Africa
				add_state_core = 964 #Amboland
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #liberate
		name = annex.193.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = NMB }
		release_targeted_tag_with_claims = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { tag = GER }
				has_socialist_government = yes
			}
			NMB = { complete_national_focus = NMB_syndicalist_liberation }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { tag = GER }
				has_authoritarian_government = yes
			}
			NMB = { complete_national_focus = NMB_stern_state }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { tag = GER }
				has_elected_government = yes
			}
			NMB = { complete_national_focus = NMB_democratic_mandate }
		}
	}

	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.occupation
		trigger = { is_ai = no }
		set_country_flag = NMB_CONQ
		occupy_medium_country = yes
	}
}

country_event = { #Annexation of Liberia
	id = annex.210
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.210" }
	title = annexation_LIB_CONQ
	desc = annexation_LIB_CONQ_desc
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			add_to_temp_array = { core_removal_array = LIB }
			remove_all_cores_and_claims_of_tags = yes
			298 = { add_core_of = LIB }
			966 = { add_core_of = LIB }
		}
	}

	option = { #liberate
		name = annex.210.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}

		trigger = {
			OR = {
				NOT = { has_government = authoritarian_democrat }
				tag = GER
				tag = MAF
			}
		}

		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					"LIB" = {
						has_cosmetic_tag = LIB_AUTHDEM
					}
				}
				"LIB" = {
					set_party_name = {
						ideology = authoritarian_democrat
						long_name = "Deutscher Liberian Bund"
						name = "DLB"
					}
				}
			}
		}

		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = LIB }
		release_targeted_tag = yes
	}

	option = { #liberate authdem (anybody but Germany and Mittelafrika)
		name = annex.210.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}

		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				tag = GER
				tag = MAF
			}
			has_government = authoritarian_democrat
		}

		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = LIB }
		release_targeted_tag = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_government = authoritarian_democrat }
				"LIB" = {
					set_cosmetic_tag = LIB_AUTHDEM
					set_party_name = {
						ideology = authoritarian_democrat
						long_name = "Authoritarian Dem."
						name = "Authoritarian Dem."
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.occupation
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		set_country_flag = LIB_CONQ
		occupy_small_country = yes
	}
}

country_event = { #Annexation of South Africa

	desc = annexation_SAF_CONQ_desc
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			SAF = {
				if = { #Clean up governor-general
					limit = {
						OR = {
							has_country_leader = { name = "Patrick Duncan" }
							has_country_leader = { name = "Nicolaas Jacobus de Wet" }
							has_country_leader = { name = "Ernest Janssen" }
							has_country_leader = { name = "George V" }
							has_country_leader = { name = "Edward VIII" }
							has_country_leader = { name = "Albert I" }
							has_country_leader = { name = "Henry IX" }
							has_country_leader = { name = "George VI" }
							has_country_leader = { name = "George Villiers" }
						}
					}
					kill_country_leader = yes
				}
				remove_ideas = SAF_wavering_dominion
				remove_ideas = SAF_neutral_dominion
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = { is_core_of = SFR }
				remove_core_of = SFR
				if = {
					limit = { is_claimed_by = SAF }
					remove_claim_by = SAF
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { is_core_of = SAF } }
					add_core_of = SAF
				}
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = { is_claimed_by = SFR }
				remove_claim_by = SFR
			}
			clr_global_flag = saf_boer_war
		}
	}

	option = { #Liberate South Africa with the protectorates
		name = annex.219.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_socialist_government = yes
					tag = MAF
					tag = GER
					tag = GEX
				}
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				owns_state = 542
				owns_state = 545
			}
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 542
					state = 545
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_claimed_by = SAF }
				remove_claim_by = SAF
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { is_core_of = SAF } }
				add_core_of = SAF
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = SAF }
		release_targeted_tag = yes
		SAF_puppet_setup = yes
	}

	option = { #liberate a simple South Africa
		name = annex.219.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 60
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 542
					state = 545
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_claimed_by = SAF }
				remove_claim_by = SAF
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_core_of = SAF }

			}

				}
			}

country_event = { # The fate of an unified central America
	id = annex.255
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.255" }
	title = annexation_CEN_CONQ
	desc = annexation_CEN_CONQ_desc

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Release a loyal unified central America
		name = annex.255.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = CEN_conquered_release
		if = {
			limit = {
				owns_state = 316
			}
			CEN_renounce_white_ruling = yes
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_state = { #Coring
				limit = {
					NOT = { is_core_of = CEN }
					OR = {
						state = 311
						state = 1071
						is_core_of = GUA
						is_core_of = ELS
						is_core_of = HON
						is_core_of = NIC
						AND = {
							is_core_of = COS
							OR = {
								COS = {
									is_subject_of = ROOT
								}
								316 = {
									is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
				add_core_of = CEN
			}

			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = CEN
					is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
				}
				CEN = {
					transfer_state = PREV
				}
			}
			set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = CEN }
			puppet_released_tag = yes
			CEN = {
				clr_country_flag = CEN_centro_released
				if = {
					limit = {
						ROOT = {
							has_socialist_government = yes
						}
					}
					load_focus_tree = Centroamerica_focus #Loads the Commie tree
					set_country_flag = CEN_centro_released
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						ROOT = {
							has_elected_government = yes
						}
					}
					load_focus_tree = CA_DEM_focus
					set_cosmetic_tag = CEN_CON
					set_party_name = {
						ideology = social_democrat
						name = CEN_social_democrat_liberal
						long_name = CEN_social_democrat_liberal
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						ROOT = {
							has_authoritarian_government = yes
						}
					}
					set_cosmetic_tag = CEN_REP
					load_focus_tree = CA_military_focus
				}

				if = {
					limit = {
						HON = {
							exists = yes
							is_subject_of = ROOT
						}
					}
					annex_country = {
						target = HON
						transfer_troops = no
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						GUA = {
							exists = yes
							is_subject_of = ROOT
						}
					}
					annex_country = {
						target = GUA
						transfer_troops = no
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NIC = {
							exists = yes
							is_subject_of = ROOT
						}
					}
					annex_country = {
						target = NIC
						transfer_troops = no
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						ELS = {
							exists = yes
							is_subject_of = ROOT
						}
					}
					annex_country = {
						target = ELS
						transfer_troops = no
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						country_exists = COS
						OR = {
							COS = {
								is_subject_of = ROOT
							}
							owns_state = 316
						}
					}
					annex_country = {
						target = COS
						transfer_troops = no
					}
				}
			}
			CEN_setleaders = yes
		}
	}

	option = { # Release every nation separately
		name = annex.255.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = release_cen_seperate
		if = {
			limit = {
				owns_state = 316
			}
			CEN_renounce_white_ruling = yes
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					owns_state = 316
					COS = {
						exists = no
					}
				}
				set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = COS }
				release_targeted_tag = yes
			}

			set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = GUA }
			release_targeted_tag = yes
			if = {
				limit = {
					GUA = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
					311 = {
						is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT
						is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
					}
				}
				GUA = {
					transfer_state = 311
					add_state_claim = 311
				}
			}
			GUA_setleaders = yes

			set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = NIC }
			release_targeted_tag = yes

			if = {
				limit = {
					1071 = {
						is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT
					}
				}
				NIC = {
					transfer_state = 1071
					add_state_claim = 1071
				}
			}
			NIC_setleaders = yes

			set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = HON }
			release_targeted_tag = yes
			HON_setleaders = yes

			set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = ELS }
			release_targeted_tag = yes
			ELS_setleaders = yes
		}
	}
	option = { # Keep it annexed
		name = annex.255.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owns_state = 316
			}
			CEN_renounce_white_ruling = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_global_flag = centroamerica_formed
					has_global_flag = demcen_formed
					has_global_flag = milcen_formed
				}
			}
			occupy_medium_country = yes
			set_country_flag = CEN_CONQ
			set_country_flag = CEN_CONQ2
		}
		else = {
			hidden_effect = {
				set_variable = {
					to_pay = 0
				}
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = GUA_CONQ
					country_exists = GUA
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				to_pay = 1
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = HON_CONQ
					country_exists = HON
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				to_pay = 1
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = ELS_CONQ
					country_exists = ELS
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				to_pay = 1
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = NIC_CONQ
					country_exists = NIC
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				to_pay = 1
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = COS_CONQ
						COS = {
							is_subject_of = ROOT
						}
					}
					316 = {
						is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				to_pay = 1
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					to_pay > 4
				}
			}
			occupy_large_country = yes
			set_country_flag = CEN_CONQ
			set_country_flag = CEN_CONQ2
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					to_pay > 2
				}
			}
			occupy_medium_country = yes
			set_country_flag = CEN_CONQ
			set_country_flag = CEN_CONQ2
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					to_pay > 0
				}
			}
			occupy_small_country = yes
			set_country_flag = CEN_CONQ
			set_country_flag = CEN_CONQ2
		}
	}
}

			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_claimed_by = ROOT }
				remove_claim_by = ROOT
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { is_core_of = ROOT } }
				add_core_of = ROOT
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #annex
		name = annex.17.h
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				tag = GRE
				tag = BUL
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1000
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
				OR = {
					state = 773
					state = 341
				}
			}
			add_claim_by = ROOT
		}
	}
	option = { #occupation
		name = annex.occupation
		trigger = {
			is_ai = no
			NOT = {
				tag = GRE
				tag = BUL
				tag = OTT
				tag = TUR

		}

		}

				}

					region = 149 #Eastern Siberia
					state = 644 #Northeast Siberia

			}
		}

			limit = {
				OR = {
					region = 148 #Outer Manchuria

					state = 563 #Chita
					state = 564 #Verkhneudinsk

				}
				is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no
			}
			TRM = {

			}

		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = TRM }
		puppet_released_tag = yes
		hidden_effect = { puppet_TRM_setup = yes }

country_event = { #The Fate of Italy

	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.280" }
	title = annexation_ITA_CONQ
	desc = annexation_ITA_CONQ_desc

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = ITA_CONQ
			if = {
				limit = { tag = AUS }
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							state = 783 #Trentino
							state = 39 #Southern Tyrol
							state = 736 #Austrian Littoral
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = { is_core_of = ITA }
						remove_core_of = ITA
						add_claim_by = ITA
					}
					if = {
						limit = { is_core_of = SRI }
						remove_core_of = SRI
						add_claim_by = SRI
					}
					if = {
						limit = { is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes }
						add_claim_by = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = annex.280.a #Release as Italy
		trigger = {
			has_socialist_government = no
			NOT = {
				tag = AUS
				has_government = authoritarian_democrat
				country_exists = ITA
				ITA = { is_ally_of_ROOT = yes }
				SRI = { is_ally_of_ROOT = yes }
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 95
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					SIC = { is_ally_of_ROOT = yes }
					SRD = { is_ally_of_ROOT = yes }
				}
			}

		}
		clr_country_flag = ITA_CONQ


		# restore initial cores if they were removed
		hidden_effect = {
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						state = 159 #Lombardy
						state = 160 #Venice
						state = 759 #Friuli
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { is_claimed_by = ITA }
					remove_claim_by = ITA
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { is_core_of = ITA } }
					add_core_of = ITA
				}
			}
		}

		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_european_italy = yes
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}
			ITA = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_ai = yes
				is_subject_of = ROOT
				is_italian_tag = yes
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				every_unit_leader = { set_nationality = ITA }
				every_navy_leader = { set_nationality = ITA }
				transfer_navy = { target = ITA }
			}
			ITA = {
				annex_country = { target = PREV transfer_troops = yes }
			}
		}

		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = { target = ITA modifier = KR_liberated_us }
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = ITA }
		puppet_released_tag = yes

		hidden_effect = {
			ITA = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_government = national_populist
						NOT = { has_idea = ITA_republic_federation }
						NOT = { has_completed_focus = ITA_destroy_austrian_influence }
					}
					add_ideas = ITA_republic_federation
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_government = national_populist
						NOT = { has_idea = ITA_republic_unitary }
						has_completed_focus = ITA_destroy_austrian_influence
					}
					add_ideas = ITA_republic_unitary
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_government = national_populist
						has_idea = ITA_republic_unitary
						has_completed_focus = ITA_centralized_power
					}
					remove_ideas = ITA_republic_unitary
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_government = national_populist }
						NOT = { has_idea = ITA_republic_federation }
						NOT = {
							has_completed_focus = ITA_nationalist_question
							has_completed_focus = ITA_stable_democracy
						}
					}
					add_ideas = ITA_republic_federation
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_idea = ITA_federation_transition }
					remove_ideas = ITA_federation_transition
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_idea = ITA_federation_secure }
					remove_ideas = ITA_federation_secure
				}
				if = {
					limit = { owns_state = 2 } #Rome
					set_capital = 2
				}
			}
		}
	}

		name = annex.280.m #Release as Italian Federation

country_event = { #Offering land in Italy in exchange for faction membership
	id = annex.281
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.281" }
	title = annex.281.t

	desc = {
		text = annex.281.d.allitaly
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = offering_italy
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = annex.281.d.centralitaly
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = offering_papacy
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = annex.281.d.piedmont
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = offering_piedmont
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = annex.281.a #We'll take the deal
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				FROM = { can_form_italy = yes }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				OR = {
					tag = PAP
					tag = SRD
				}
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = { is_in_faction = yes }
			hidden_effect = {
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						is_subject = no
						is_in_faction_with = ROOT
						NOT = { tag = ROOT }
					}
					country_event = annex.284
				}
			}
			leave_faction = yes
		}

		separate_peace_all_wars = yes

		FROM = {
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					if = {
						limit = { ROOT = { has_country_flag = offering_italy } }
						is_european_italy = yes
					}
					if = {
						limit = { ROOT = { has_country_flag = offering_papacy } }
						OR = {
							state = 764 #Viterbo
							state = 1005 #Umbria
							state = 157 #Marche
							state = 161 #Romagna
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = { ROOT = { has_country_flag = offering_piedmont } }
						OR = {
							state = 1003 #Aosta Valley
							state = 158 #Piedmont
							state = 838 #Liguria
							state = 762 #Nice
							state = 735 #Savoy
							state = 943 #Upper Savoy
						}
					}
					is_not_claim_or_core_of_PREV = yes
				}
				ROOT = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_faction_leader = yes }
				add_to_faction = ROOT
			}
			country_event = { id = annex.282 days = 1 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = annex.281.b #We refuse
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				is_in_faction = no
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				OR = {
					has_war = yes
					tag = SIC
				}
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = { id = annex.283 days = 1 }
		}
	}
}

		}
	}

		trigger = {
			160 = { #Venice
				is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}

		}

			factor = 50
		}

						state = 759 #Friuli
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { is_claimed_by = ITA }
					remove_claim_by = ITA
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { is_core_of = ITA } }
					add_core_of = ITA
				}
			}
		}

			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 159

				}

			}

		}

			if = {

				}
			}

				if = {
					limit = {
						has_government = national_populist

					}

				}

					limit = {
						has_government = national_populist

					}

					limit = {

						has_completed_focus = ITA_centralized_power
					}
					remove_ideas = ITA_republic_unitary
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_government = national_populist }
						NOT = { has_idea = ITA_republic_federation }
						NOT = {
							has_completed_focus = ITA_nationalist_question
							has_completed_focus = ITA_stable_democracy
						}
					}
					add_ideas = ITA_republic_federation
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_idea = ITA_federation_transition }
					remove_ideas = ITA_federation_transition

					limit = { has_idea = ITA_federation_secure }
					remove_ideas = ITA_federation_secure
				}
			}
		}

		}
	}

		name = annex.289.a #Release as PAP

			has_socialist_government = no

		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_italian_tag = no

					ITA = { is_ally_of_ROOT = yes }
					SRI = { is_ally_of_ROOT = yes }
				}
			}
		}
		clr_country_flag = PAP_CONQ

			PAP = {
				add_state_core = 2

			}
		}

			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 2 #Rome

country_event = { #The Fate of Piedmont
	id = annex.291
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.291" }
	title = annexation_PIEDMONT_CONQ
	desc = annexation_PIEDMONT_CONQ_desc

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = PIEDMONT_CONQ
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = annex.280.b #Release as SRI
		trigger = {
			has_socialist_government = yes
			NOT = {
				is_italian_tag = yes
				country_exists = SRI
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_italian_tag = no
				OR = {
					ITA = { is_ally_of_ROOT = yes }
					SRI = { is_ally_of_ROOT = yes }
				}
			}
		}
		clr_country_flag = PIEDMONT_CONQ

		# restore initial cores if they were removed
		hidden_effect = {
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						state = 1003 #Aosta Valley
						state = 158 #Piedmont
						state = 838 #Liguria
						state = 1004 #Emilia
						state = 161 #Romagna
						state = 162 #Tuscany
						state = 157 #Marches
						state = 1005 #Umbria
						state = 764 #Viterbo
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { is_claimed_by = SRI }
					remove_claim_by = SRI
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { is_core_of = SRI } }
					add_core_of = SRI
				}
			}
		}

		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 1003 #Aosta Valley
					state = 158 #Piedmont
					state = 838 #Liguria
					state = 1004 #Emilia
					state = 161 #Romagna
					state = 162 #Tuscany
					state = 157 #Marches
					state = 1005 #Umbria
					state = 764 #Viterbo
					state = 762 #Nice
					state = 735 #Savoy
					state = 943 #Upper Savoy
				}
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}
			SRI = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}

		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = { target = SRI modifier = KR_liberated_us }
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = SRI }
		puppet_released_tag = yes
	}
	option = {
		name = annex.291.a #Release as SRD
		trigger = {
			has_socialist_government = no
			NOT = {
				country_exists = SRD
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_italian_tag = no
				OR = {
					ITA = { is_ally_of_ROOT = yes }
					SRI = { is_ally_of_ROOT = yes }
				}
			}
		}
		clr_country_flag = PIEDMONT_CONQ

		# restore initial cores if they were removed
		hidden_effect = {
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						state = 1002 #Sassari
						state = 114 #Cagliari
						state = 1003 #Aosta Valley
						state = 158 #Piedmont
						state = 838 #Liguria
						state = 762 #Nice
						state = 735 #Savoy
						state = 943 #Upper Savoy
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { is_claimed_by = SRD }
					remove_claim_by = SRD
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { is_core_of = SRD } }
					add_core_of = SRD
				}
			}
		}

		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 1003 #Aosta Valley
					state = 158 #Piedmont
					state = 838 #Liguria
					state = 1002 #Sassari
					state = 114 #Cagliari
				}
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}
			SRD = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}

		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = SRD }
		puppet_released_tag = yes
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = SIC_confed }
			set_autonomy = {
				target = SRD
				autonomy_state = kr_federated_state
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				SRD = {
					owns_state = 158
					NOT = { has_cosmetic_tag = SRD_piedmont }
				}
			}

			is_german_tag = no
			var:780.owner = {
				is_germany_or_splinter_tag = yes
				is_ally_with = ROOT
				NOT = { tag = var:42.owner } #avoids duplication with the next option
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				any_allied_country = {
					is_french_tag = yes
					OR = {
						owns_state = 779 #Nancy
						owns_state = 785 #Plateau Lorrain
					}
				}
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = 780.owner }
		if = {
			limit = { owns_state = 779 }
			779 = { transfer_state_and_add_core = yes }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { owns_state = 28 }
			28 = { transfer_state_and_add_core = yes }
		}
	}

	option = { #Integrate
		name = annex.17.h
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				is_french_tag = yes
				is_german_tag = yes
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = ROOT }
		if = {
			limit = { is_french_tag = yes }
			if = {
				limit = { owns_state = 779 }
				779 = { transfer_state_and_add_claim = yes }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { owns_state = 28 }
				28 = { transfer_state_and_add_claim = yes }
			}
		}
		else = {
			if = {
				limit = { owns_state = 779 }
				779 = { transfer_state_and_add_core = yes }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { owns_state = 28 }
				28 = { transfer_state_and_add_core = yes }
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = annex.occupation #Occupy
		trigger = { is_ai = no }
		set_country_flag = ALSACE_CONQ
		occupy_medium_country = yes
	}
}

country_event = { #The Fate of Corsica
	id = annex.295
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.295" }
	title = annexation_CORSICA_CONQ
	desc = annexation_CORSICA_CONQ_desc

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = annex.295.a #Give to France
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				is_in_faction_with = FRA
				is_in_faction_with = NFA
				is_in_faction_with = FRP
				FRA = {
					is_subject_of = ROOT
				}
				NFA = {
					is_subject_of = ROOT
				}
				FRP = {
					is_subject_of = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_in_faction_with = FRP
					FRP = {
						is_subject_of = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			FRP = { transfer_state = 1 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_in_faction_with = FRA
					FRA = {
						is_subject_of = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			FRA = { transfer_state = 1 }

					is_in_faction_with = NFA

		}

					}
				}
			}
			TUS = {
				add_state_core = 1

			}
		}
		else_if = {

					ITA = {
						is_subject_of = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			ITA = {
				add_state_core = 1

		else_if = {

					}
				}

country_event = {
	id = annex.296
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.296" }
	title = annexation_AST_restoring_australasia
	desc = annexation_AST_restoring_australasia_desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_AST_crowd1

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = AST
					is_claimed_by = ROOT
				}
				remove_claim_by = ROOT
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = annex.296.a #The New Guard can restore order
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 60
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				OR = {
					has_government = social_democrat
					has_government = social_liberal
				}
			}
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = AST
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
				}
			}
			AST = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		add_to_faction = AST
		AST = {
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = national_populist
				elections_allowed = no
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				set_capital = 985
				AST_enact_entente_trade = yes
				AST_remove_republic = yes
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							has_idea = AST_new_unrest
						}
					}
					add_ideas = AST_new_unrest
				}
				country_event = austral.248
				remove_all_ministers = yes
				add_ideas = {
					AST_William_JR_Scott_hog_npo
					AST_John_F_Dynon_for_npo
					AST_Hubert_L_Primrose_eco_npo

						name = "Thomas Blamey"
						picture = "Portrait_AST_Thomas_Blamey.tga"

							old_guard
							politically_connected
							war_hero
							organizer
							thorough_planner
						}

						attack_skill = 4
						defense_skill = 3
						planning_skill = 3
						logistics_skill = 3
						id = 2100
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				has_authoritarian_government = yes
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -100
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = AST
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
				}
			}
			AST = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = AST }
		puppet_released_tag = yes
		AST = {
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = authoritarian_democrat
				elections_allowed = no
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				set_capital = 985
				AST_enact_entente_trade = yes

			}

		}

				SIC = {

				}

					exists = yes

				exists = yes
				OR = {
					is_in_faction_with = ROOT
					is_subject_of = ROOT
				}
			}
		}

		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = SAR
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}
			add_core_of = MAL
			MAL = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
	}

	option = { #Give it to the Insulindians
		name = annex.299.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 80
		}
		trigger = {
			INS = {
				exists = yes
				OR = {
					is_in_faction_with = ROOT
					is_subject_of = ROOT
				}
			}
		}

		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = SAR
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}
			INS = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
	}

	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.occupation
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		set_country_flag = SAR_CONQ
		occupy_small_country = yes
	}
}
